I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Add support for spreading non-string attribute values in templ.RenderAttributes
**Describe the bug**

Since merging #1129 it's allowed to do something like this

```
<input type="text" value={ val } />
```

where `val` is an `int`. It will get converted automatically and rendered as

```
<input type="text" value="42">
```

However, if I do this

```
{{ attr := templ.Attributes{"type": "text, "value": 42} }}
<input { attr... } />
```

only the `type` attribute will get rendered:

```
<input type="text">
```

The culprit seems to be `RenderAttributes` in `runtime.go`, which in its `switch` statement only type-checks for `string`, `*string`, `bool`, `*bool`, `KeyValue[string, bool]`, `KeyValue[bool, bool]` and `func() bool`.

**Expected behavior**

I'd expect attribute values stored in `templ.Attributes` (which is a `map[string]any` after all) to be treated the same as if I had specified them directly, that is passed through `fmt.Sprint` or something.

**`templ info` output**

```
(✓) os [ goos=linux goarch=amd64 ]
(✓) go [ location=/usr/local/go/bin/go version=go version go1.25rc1 linux/amd64 ]

(✓) templ [ location=/home/chris/.local/bin/templ version=v0.3.906 ]
```

</pr_description>

    28	}

    30	// ComponentFunc converts a function that matches the Component interface's

    41	        ctx, v := getContext(ctx)

    43	        return ctx

    46	// GetNonce returns the CSP nonce value set with WithNonce, or an

    49	        if ctx == nil {
    50	                return ""

    99	// String returns the names of all CSS classes.
   100	func (classes CSSClasses) String() string {
   101	        if len(classes) == 0 {
   102	                return ""
   103	        }
   104	        cp := newCSSProcessor()
   105	        for _, v := range classes {
   106	                cp.Add(v)
   107	        }
   108	        return cp.String()
   109	}
   110	
   111	func newCSSProcessor() *cssProcessor {
   112	        return &cssProcessor{
   113	                classNameToEnabled: make(map[string]bool),
   114	        }
   115	}
   116	
   117	type cssProcessor struct {
   118	        classNameToEnabled map[string]bool
   119	        orderedNames       []string
   120	}
   121	
   122	func (cp *cssProcessor) Add(item any) {
   123	        switch c := item.(type) {
   124	        case []string:
   125	                for _, className := range c {
   126	                        cp.AddClassName(className, true)
   127	                }
   128	        case string:
   129	                cp.AddClassName(c, true)
   130	        case ConstantCSSClass:
   131	                cp.AddClassName(c.ClassName(), true)
   132	        case ComponentCSSClass:
   133	                cp.AddClassName(c.ClassName(), true)
   134	        case map[string]bool:
   135	                // In Go, map keys are iterated in a randomized order.
   136	                // So the keys in the map must be sorted to produce consistent output.
   137	                keys := make([]string, len(c))
   138	                var i int
   139	                for key := range c {
   140	                        keys[i] = key
   141	                        i++
   142	                }
   143	                sort.Strings(keys)
   144	                for _, className := range keys {
   145	                        cp.AddClassName(className, c[className])
   146	                }
   147	        case []KeyValue[string, bool]:
   148	                for _, kv := range c {
   149	                        cp.AddClassName(kv.Key, kv.Value)
   150	                }
   151	        case KeyValue[string, bool]:
   152	                cp.AddClassName(c.Key, c.Value)
   153	        case []KeyValue[CSSClass, bool]:
   154	                for _, kv := range c {
   155	                        cp.AddClassName(kv.Key.ClassName(), kv.Value)
   156	                }
   157	        case KeyValue[CSSClass, bool]:
   158	                cp.AddClassName(c.Key.ClassName(), c.Value)
   159	        case CSSClasses:
   160	                for _, item := range c {
   161	                        cp.Add(item)
   162	                }
   163	        case []CSSClass:
   164	                for _, item := range c {
   165	                        cp.Add(item)
   166	                }
   167	        case func() CSSClass:
   168	                cp.AddClassName(c().ClassName(), true)
   169	        default:
   170	                cp.AddClassName(unknownTypeClassName, true)
   171	        }
   172	}
   173	
   174	func (cp *cssProcessor) AddClassName(className string, enabled bool) {
   175	        cp.classNameToEnabled[className] = enabled
   176	        cp.orderedNames = append(cp.orderedNames, className)
   177	}
   178	
   179	func (cp *cssProcessor) String() string {
   180	        // Order the outputs according to how they were input, and remove disabled names.
   181	        rendered := make(map[string]any, len(cp.classNameToEnabled))
   182	        var names []string
   183	        for _, name := range cp.orderedNames {
   184	                if enabled := cp.classNameToEnabled[name]; !enabled {
   185	                        continue
   186	                }
   187	                if _, hasBeenRendered := rendered[name]; hasBeenRendered {
   188	                        continue
   189	                }
   190	                names = append(names, name)
   191	                rendered[name] = struct{}{}
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        return strings.Join(names, " ")
   195	}
   196	
   197	// KeyValue is a key and value pair.
   198	type KeyValue[TKey comparable, TValue any] struct {
   199	        Key   TKey   `json:"name"`
   200	        Value TValue `json:"value"`
   201	}
   202	
   203	// KV creates a new key/value pair from the input key and value.
   204	func KV[TKey comparable, TValue any](key TKey, value TValue) KeyValue[TKey, TValue] {
   205	        return KeyValue[TKey, TValue]{
   206	                Key:   key,
   207	                Value: value,
   208	        }
   209	}
   210	
   211	const unknownTypeClassName = "--templ-css-class-unknown-type"
   212	
   213	// Class returns a CSS class name.
   214	// Deprecated: use a string instead.
   215	func Class(name string) CSSClass {
   216	        return SafeClass(name)
   217	}
   218	
   219	// SafeClass bypasses CSS class name validation.
   220	// Deprecated: use a string instead.
   221	func SafeClass(name string) CSSClass {
   222	        return ConstantCSSClass(name)
   223	}
   224	
   225	// CSSClass provides a class name.
   226	type CSSClass interface {
   227	        ClassName() string
   228	}
   229	
   230	// ConstantCSSClass is a string constant of a CSS class name.
   231	// Deprecated: use a string instead.
   232	type ConstantCSSClass string
   233	
   234	// ClassName of the CSS class.
   235	func (css ConstantCSSClass) ClassName() string {
   236	        return string(css)
   237	}
   238	
   239	// ComponentCSSClass is a templ.CSS
   240	type ComponentCSSClass struct {
   241	        // ID of the class, will be autogenerated.
   242	        ID string
   243	        // Definition of the CSS.
   244	        Class SafeCSS
   245	}
   246	
   247	// ClassName of the CSS class.
   248	func (css ComponentCSSClass) ClassName() string {
   249	        return css.ID
   250	}
   251	
   252	// CSSID calculates an ID.
   253	func CSSID(name string, css string) string {
   254	        sum := sha256.Sum256([]byte(css))
   255	        hs := hex.EncodeToString(sum[:])[0:8] // NOTE: See issue #978. Minimum recommended hs length is 6.
   256	        // Benchmarking showed this was fastest, and with fewest allocations (1).
   257	        // Using strings.Builder (2 allocs).
   258	        // Using fmt.Sprintf (3 allocs).
   259	        return name + "_" + hs
   260	}
   261	
   262	// NewCSSMiddleware creates HTTP middleware that renders a global stylesheet of ComponentCSSClass
   263	// CSS if the request path matches, or updates the HTTP context to ensure that any handlers that
   264	// use templ.Components skip rendering <style> elements for classes that are included in the global
   265	// stylesheet. By default, the stylesheet path is /styles/templ.css
   266	func NewCSSMiddleware(next http.Handler, classes ...CSSClass) CSSMiddleware {
   267	        return CSSMiddleware{
   268	                Path:       "/styles/templ.css",
   269	                CSSHandler: NewCSSHandler(classes...),
   270	                Next:       next,
   271	        }
   272	}
   273	
   274	// CSSMiddleware renders a global stylesheet.
   275	type CSSMiddleware struct {
   276	        Path       string
   277	        CSSHandler CSSHandler
   278	        Next       http.Handler
   279	}
   280	
   281	func (cssm CSSMiddleware) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   282	        if r.URL.Path == cssm.Path {
   283	                cssm.CSSHandler.ServeHTTP(w, r)
   284	                return
   285	        }
   286	        // Add registered classes to the context.
   287	        ctx, v := getContext(r.Context())
   288	        for _, c := range cssm.CSSHandler.Classes {
   289	                v.addClass(c.ID)
   290	        }
   291	        // Serve the request. Templ components will use the updated context
   292	        // to know to skip rendering <style> elements for any component CSS
   293	        // classes that have been included in the global stylesheet.
   294	        cssm.Next.ServeHTTP(w, r.WithContext(ctx))
   295	}
   296	
   297	// NewCSSHandler creates a handler that serves a stylesheet containing the CSS of the
   298	// classes passed in. This is used by the CSSMiddleware to provide global stylesheets
   299	// for templ components.
   300	func NewCSSHandler(classes ...CSSClass) CSSHandler {
   301	        ccssc := make([]ComponentCSSClass, 0, len(classes))
   302	        for _, c := range classes {
   303	                ccss, ok := c.(ComponentCSSClass)
   304	                if !ok {
   305	                        continue
   306	                }
   307	                ccssc = append(ccssc, ccss)
   308	        }
   309	        return CSSHandler{
   310	                Classes: ccssc,
   311	        }
   312	}
   313	
   314	// CSSHandler is a HTTP handler that serves CSS.
   315	type CSSHandler struct {
   316	        Logger  func(err error)
   317	        Classes []ComponentCSSClass
   318	}
   319	
   320	func (cssh CSSHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   321	        w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/css")
   322	        for _, c := range cssh.Classes {
   323	                _, err := w.Write([]byte(c.Class))
   324	                if err != nil && cssh.Logger != nil {
   325	                        cssh.Logger(err)
   326	                }
   327	        }
   328	}
   329	
   330	// RenderCSSItems renders the CSS to the writer, if the items haven't already been rendered.
   331	func RenderCSSItems(ctx context.Context, w io.Writer, classes ...any) (err error) {
   332	        if len(classes) == 0 {
   333	                return nil
   334	        }
   335	        _, v := getContext(ctx)
   336	        sb := new(strings.Builder)
   337	        renderCSSItemsToBuilder(sb, v, classes...)
   338	        if sb.Len() == 0 {
   339	                return nil
   340	        }
   341	        if _, err = io.WriteString(w, `<style type="text/css"`); err != nil {
   342	                return err
   343	        }
   344	        if v.nonce != "" {
   345	                if err = writeStrings(w, ` nonce="`, EscapeString(v.nonce), `"`); err != nil {
   346	                        return err
   347	                }
   348	        }
   349	        return writeStrings(w, `>`, sb.String(), `</style>`)
   350	}
   351	
   352	func renderCSSItemsToBuilder(sb *strings.Builder, v *contextValue, classes ...any) {
   353	        for _, c := range classes {
   354	                switch ccc := c.(type) {
   355	                case ComponentCSSClass:
   356	                        if !v.hasClassBeenRendered(ccc.ID) {
   357	                                sb.WriteString(string(ccc.Class))
   358	                                v.addClass(ccc.ID)
   359	                        }
   360	                case KeyValue[ComponentCSSClass, bool]:
   361	                        if !ccc.Value {
   362	                                continue
   363	                        }
   364	                        renderCSSItemsToBuilder(sb, v, ccc.Key)
   365	                case KeyValue[CSSClass, bool]:
   366	                        if !ccc.Value {
   367	                                continue
   368	                        }
   369	                        renderCSSItemsToBuilder(sb, v, ccc.Key)
   370	                case CSSClasses:
   371	                        renderCSSItemsToBuilder(sb, v, ccc...)
   372	                case []CSSClass:
   373	                        for _, item := range ccc {
   374	                                renderCSSItemsToBuilder(sb, v, item)
   375	                        }
   376	                case func() CSSClass:
   377	                        renderCSSItemsToBuilder(sb, v, ccc())
   378	                case []string:
   379	                        // Skip. These are class names, not CSS classes.
   380	                case string:
   381	                        // Skip. This is a class name, not a CSS class.
   382	                case ConstantCSSClass:
   383	                        // Skip. This is a class name, not a CSS class.
   384	                case CSSClass:
   385	                        // Skip. This is a class name, not a CSS class.
   386	                case map[string]bool:
   387	                        // Skip. These are class names, not CSS classes.
   388	                case KeyValue[string, bool]:
   389	                        // Skip. These are class names, not CSS classes.
   390	                case []KeyValue[string, bool]:
   391	                        // Skip. These are class names, not CSS classes.
   392	                case KeyValue[ConstantCSSClass, bool]:
   393	                        // Skip. These are class names, not CSS classes.
   394	                case []KeyValue[ConstantCSSClass, bool]:
   395	                        // Skip. These are class names, not CSS classes.
   396	                }
   397	        }
   398	}
   399	
   400	// SafeCSS is CSS that has been sanitized.
   401	type SafeCSS string
   402	
   403	type SafeCSSProperty string
   404	
   405	var safeCSSPropertyType = reflect.TypeOf(SafeCSSProperty(""))
   406	
   407	// SanitizeCSS sanitizes CSS properties to ensure that they are safe.
   408	func SanitizeCSS[T ~string](property string, value T) SafeCSS {
   409	        if reflect.TypeOf(value) == safeCSSPropertyType {
   410	                return SafeCSS(safehtml.SanitizeCSSProperty(property) + ":" + string(value) + ";")
   411	        }
   412	        p, v := safehtml.SanitizeCSS(property, string(value))
   413	        return SafeCSS(p + ":" + v + ";")
   414	}
   415	
   416	type Attributer interface {
   417	        Items() []KeyValue[string, any]
   418	}
   419	
   420	// Attributes is an alias to map[string]any made for spread attributes.
   421	type Attributes map[string]any
   422	
   423	var _ Attributer = Attributes{}
   424	
   425	// Returns the items of the attributes map in key sorted order.
   426	func (a Attributes) Items() []KeyValue[string, any] {
   427	        var (
   428	                items = make([]KeyValue[string, any], len(a))
   429	                i     int
   430	        )
   431	        for k, v := range a {
   432	                items[i] = KeyValue[string, any]{Key: k, Value: v}
   433	                i++
   434	        }
   435	        sort.Slice(items, func(i, j int) bool {
   436	                return items[i].Key < items[j].Key
   437	        })
   438	        return items
   439	}
   440	
   441	// OrderedAttributes stores attributes in order of insertion.
   442	type OrderedAttributes []KeyValue[string, any]
   443	
   444	var _ Attributer = OrderedAttributes{}
   445	
   446	func (a OrderedAttributes) Items() []KeyValue[string, any] {
   447	        return a
   448	}
   449	
   450	func writeStrings(w io.Writer, ss ...string) (err error) {
   451	        for _, s := range ss {
   452	                if _, err = io.WriteString(w, s); err != nil {
   453	                        return err
   454	                }
   455	        }
   456	        return nil
   457	}
   458	
   459	func RenderAttributes(ctx context.Context, w io.Writer, attributes Attributer) (err error) {
   460	        for _, item := range attributes.Items() {
   461	                key := item.Key
   462	                value := item.Value
   463	                switch value := value.(type) {
   464	                case string:
   465	                        if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(value), `"`); err != nil {
   466	                                return err
   467	                        }
   468	                case *string:
   469	                        if value != nil {
   470	                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(*value), `"`); err != nil {
   471	                                        return err
   472	                                }
   473	                        }
   474	                case bool:
   475	                        if value {
   476	                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
   477	                                        return err
   478	                                }
   479	                        }
   480	                case *bool:
   481	                        if value != nil && *value {
   482	                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
   483	                                        return err
   484	                                }
   485	                        }
   486	                case KeyValue[string, bool]:
   487	                        if value.Value {
   488	                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(value.Key), `"`); err != nil {
   489	                                        return err
   490	                                }
   491	                        }
   492	                case KeyValue[bool, bool]:
   493	                        if value.Value && value.Key {
   494	                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
   495	                                        return err
   496	                                }
   497	                        }
   498	                case func() bool:
   499	                        if value() {
   500	                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
   501	                                        return err
   502	                                }
   503	                        }
   504	                }
   505	        }
   506	        return nil
   507	}

   522	func (v *contextValue) setHasBeenRendered(h *OnceHandle) {
   523	        if v.onceHandles == nil {
   524	                v.onceHandles = map[*OnceHandle]struct{}{}
   525	        }
   526	        v.onceHandles[h] = struct{}{}
   527	}
   528	
   529	func (v *contextValue) getHasBeenRendered(h *OnceHandle) (ok bool) {
   530	        if v.onceHandles == nil {
   531	                v.onceHandles = map[*OnceHandle]struct{}{}
   532	        }
   533	        _, ok = v.onceHandles[h]
   534	        return
   535	}
   536	
   537	func (v *contextValue) addScript(s string) {
   538	        if v.ss == nil {
   539	                v.ss = map[string]struct{}{}
   540	        }
   541	        v.ss["script_"+s] = struct{}{}
   542	}
   543	
   544	func (v *contextValue) hasScriptBeenRendered(s string) (ok bool) {
   545	        if v.ss == nil {
   546	                v.ss = map[string]struct{}{}
   547	        }
   548	        _, ok = v.ss["script_"+s]
   549	        return
   550	}
   551	
   552	func (v *contextValue) addClass(s string) {
   553	        if v.ss == nil {
   554	                v.ss = map[string]struct{}{}
   555	        }
   556	        v.ss["class_"+s] = struct{}{}
   557	}
   558	
   559	func (v *contextValue) hasClassBeenRendered(s string) (ok bool) {
   560	        if v.ss == nil {
   561	                v.ss = map[string]struct{}{}
   562	        }
   563	        _, ok = v.ss["class_"+s]
   564	        return
   565	}
   566	
   567	// InitializeContext initializes context used to store internal state used during rendering.
   568	func InitializeContext(ctx context.Context) context.Context {
   569	        if _, ok := ctx.Value(contextKey).(*contextValue); ok {
   570	                return ctx
   571	        }
   572	        v := &contextValue{}
   573	        ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, contextKey, v)
   574	        return ctx
   575	}
   576	
   577	func getContext(ctx context.Context) (context.Context, *contextValue) {
   578	        v, ok := ctx.Value(contextKey).(*contextValue)
   579	        if !ok {
   580	                ctx = InitializeContext(ctx)
   581	                v = ctx.Value(contextKey).(*contextValue)
   582	        }
   583	        return ctx, v
   584	}

   586	var bufferPool = sync.Pool{
   587	        New: func() any {
   588	                return new(bytes.Buffer)
   589	        },
   590	}
   591	
   592	func GetBuffer() *bytes.Buffer {
   593	        return bufferPool.Get().(*bytes.Buffer)
   594	}
   595	
   596	func ReleaseBuffer(b *bytes.Buffer) {
   597	        b.Reset()
   598	        bufferPool.Put(b)
   599	}

   621	// JoinStringErrs joins an optional list of errors.
   622	func JoinStringErrs[T stringable](s T, errs ...error) (string, error) {
   623	        return fmt.Sprint(s), errors.Join(errs...)
   624	}

   626	// Error returned during template rendering.
   627	type Error struct {
   628	        Err error
   629	        // FileName of the template file.
   630	        FileName string
   631	        // Line index of the error.
   632	        Line int
   633	        // Col index of the error.
   634	        Col int
   635	}
   636	
   637	func (e Error) Error() string {
   638	        if e.FileName == "" {
   639	                e.FileName = "templ"
   640	        }
   641	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s: error at line %d, col %d: %v", e.FileName, e.Line, e.Col, e.Err)
   642	}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_nonstring_attrs.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test script to reproduce the issue with non-string attribute values in templ.Attributes"""

import subprocess
import tempfile
import os

test_content = """package test

import (
    "context"
    "fmt"
    "strings"
    "testing"

    "github.com/a-h/templ"
)

func TestNonStringAttributes(t *testing.T) {
    // Test with integer attribute value
    attrs := templ.Attributes{
        "type": "text",
        "value": 42,
    }
    
    var buf strings.Builder
    err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, attrs)
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("RenderAttributes failed: %v", err)
    }
    
    result := buf.String()
    expected := ` type="text" value="42"`
    if result != expected {
        t.Errorf("Expected %q but got %q", expected, result)
    }
    
    fmt.Printf("Test Result: %q\n", result)
    fmt.Printf("Expected: %q\n", expected)
}

func main() {
    t := &testing.T{}
    TestNonStringAttributes(t)
}
"""

def main():
    # Create a temporary Go file
    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(mode='"'"'w'"'"', suffix='"'"'_test.go'"'"', delete=False) as f:
        f.write(test_content)
        temp_file = f.name
    
    try:
        # Change to testbed directory and run the test
        os.chdir('"'"'/testbed'"'"')
        result = subprocess.run(['"'"'go'"'"', '"'"'test'"'"', '"'"'-v'"'"', temp_file], 
                              capture_output=True, text=True)
        
        print("STDOUT:")
        print(result.stdout)
        print("\nSTDERR:")
        print(result.stderr)
        print(f"\nReturn code: {result.returncode}")
        
    finally:
        # Clean up
        os.unlink(temp_file)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()'

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/a-h/templ"
)

func main() {
	// Test with integer attribute value
	attrs := templ.Attributes{
		"type":  "text",
		"value": 42,
	}
	
	var buf strings.Builder
	err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, attrs)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("RenderAttributes failed: %v\n", err)
		return
	}
	
	result := buf.String()
	expected := ` type="text" value="42"`
	
	fmt.Printf("Test Result: %q\n", result)
	fmt.Printf("Expected: %q\n", expected)
	
	if result == expected {
		fmt.Println("✓ Test PASSED")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Test FAILED")
	}
}'

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/a-h/templ"
)

func main() {
	// Test with integer attribute value
	attrs := templ.Attributes{
		"type":  "text",
		"value": 42,
	}
	
	var buf strings.Builder
	err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, attrs)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("RenderAttributes failed: %v\n", err)
		return
	}
	
	result := buf.String()
	expected := ` type="text" value="42"`
	
	fmt.Printf("Test Result: %q\n", result)
	fmt.Printf("Expected: %q\n", expected)
	
	if result == expected {
		fmt.Println("✓ Test PASSED")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Test FAILED")
	}
}'

import (
	"context"

	"strings"

)

func main() {
	// Test with integer attribute value
	attrs := templ.Attributes{
		"type":  "text",
		"value": 42,
	}
	
	var buf strings.Builder
	err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, attrs)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("RenderAttributes failed: %v\n", err)
		return
	}
	
	result := buf.String()
	expected := ` type="text" value="42"`
	
	fmt.Printf("Test Result: %q\n", result)
	fmt.Printf("Expected: %q\n", expected)
	
	if result == expected {
		fmt.Println("✓ Test PASSED")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("✗ Test FAILED")
	}
}'

     9	func TestGeneratedTemplate(t *testing.T) {
    10	        f := func(input GeneratedComponentInput) error {
    11	                _, err := input.Writer.Write([]byte("Hello, World!"))
    12	                return err
    13	        }
    14	        sb := new(strings.Builder)
    15	        err := GeneratedTemplate(f).Render(context.Background(), sb)
    16	        if err != nil {
    17	                t.Errorf("unexpected error: %v", err)
    18	        }

    18	func TestCSSID(t *testing.T) {
    19	        t.Run("minimum hash suffix length is 8", func(t *testing.T) {
    20	                // See issue #978.
    21	                name := "classA"
    22	                css := "background-color:white;"
    23	                actual := len(templ.CSSID(name, css))
    24	                expected := len(name) + 1 + 8
    25	                if expected != actual {
    26	                        t.Errorf("expected length %d, got %d", expected, actual)
    27	                }
    28	        })
    29	        t.Run("known hash collisions are avoided", func(t *testing.T) {
    30	                name := "classA"
    31	                // Note that the first 4 characters of the hash are the same.
    32	                css1 := "grid-column:1;grid-row:1;"  // After hash: f781266f
    33	                css2 := "grid-column:13;grid-row:6;" // After hash: f781f18b
    34	                id1 := templ.CSSID(name, css1)
    35	                id2 := templ.CSSID(name, css2)
    36	                if id1 == id2 {
    37	                        t.Errorf("hash collision: %s == %s", id1, id2)
    38	                }
    39	        })
    40	}

    42	func TestCSSHandler(t *testing.T) {
    43	        tests := []struct {
    44	                name             string
    45	                input            []templ.CSSClass
    46	                expectedMIMEType string
    47	                expectedBody     string
    48	        }{
    49	                {
    50	                        name:             "no classes",
    51	                        input:            nil,
    52	                        expectedMIMEType: "text/css",
    53	                        expectedBody:     "",
    54	                },
    55	                {
    56	                        name:             "classes are rendered",
    57	                        input:            []templ.CSSClass{templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "className", Class: templ.SafeCSS(".className{background-color:white;}")}},
    58	                        expectedMIMEType: "text/css",
    59	                        expectedBody:     ".className{background-color:white;}",
    60	                },
    61	                {
    62	                        name: "classes are rendered",
    63	                        input: []templ.CSSClass{
    64	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "classA", Class: templ.SafeCSS(".classA{background-color:white;}")},
    65	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "classB", Class: templ.SafeCSS(".classB{background-color:green;}")},
    66	                        },
    67	                        expectedMIMEType: "text/css",
    68	                        expectedBody:     ".classA{background-color:white;}.classB{background-color:green;}",
    69	                },
    70	        }
    71	        for _, tt := range tests {
    72	                tt := tt
    73	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
    74	                        w := httptest.NewRecorder()
    75	                        h := templ.NewCSSHandler(tt.input...)
    76	                        h.ServeHTTP(w, &http.Request{})
    77	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(tt.expectedMIMEType, w.Header().Get("Content-Type")); diff != "" {
    78	                                t.Error(diff)
    79	                        }
    80	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(tt.expectedBody, w.Body.String()); diff != "" {
    81	                                t.Error(diff)
    82	                        }
    83	                })
    84	        }
    85	}

    87	func TestCSSMiddleware(t *testing.T) {
    88	        pageHandler := http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    89	                if _, err := io.WriteString(w, "Hello, World!"); err != nil {
    90	                        t.Fatalf("failed to write string: %v", err)
    91	                }
    92	        })
    93	        c1 := templ.ComponentCSSClass{
    94	                ID:    "c1",
    95	                Class: ".c1{color:red}",
    96	        }
    97	        c2 := templ.ComponentCSSClass{
    98	                ID:    "c2",
    99	                Class: ".c2{color:blue}",
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        tests := []struct {
   103	                name             string
   104	                input            *http.Request
   105	                handler          http.Handler
   106	                expectedMIMEType string
   107	                expectedBody     string
   108	        }{
   109	                {
   110	                        name:             "accessing /style/templ.css renders CSS, even if it's empty",
   111	                        input:            httptest.NewRequest("GET", "/styles/templ.css", nil),
   112	                        handler:          templ.NewCSSMiddleware(pageHandler),
   113	                        expectedMIMEType: "text/css",
   114	                        expectedBody:     "",
   115	                },
   116	                {
   117	                        name:             "accessing /style/templ.css renders CSS that includes the classes",
   118	                        input:            httptest.NewRequest("GET", "/styles/templ.css", nil),
   119	                        handler:          templ.NewCSSMiddleware(pageHandler, c1, c2),
   120	                        expectedMIMEType: "text/css",
   121	                        expectedBody:     ".c1{color:red}.c2{color:blue}",
   122	                },
   123	                {
   124	                        name:             "the pageHandler is rendered",
   125	                        input:            httptest.NewRequest("GET", "/index.html", nil),
   126	                        handler:          templ.NewCSSMiddleware(pageHandler, c1, c2),
   127	                        expectedMIMEType: "text/plain; charset=utf-8",
   128	                        expectedBody:     "Hello, World!",
   129	                },
   130	        }
   131	        for _, tt := range tests {
   132	                tt := tt
   133	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   134	                        w := httptest.NewRecorder()
   135	                        tt.handler.ServeHTTP(w, tt.input)
   136	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(tt.expectedMIMEType, w.Header().Get("Content-Type")); diff != "" {
   137	                                t.Error(diff)
   138	                        }
   139	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(tt.expectedBody, w.Body.String()); diff != "" {
   140	                                t.Error(diff)
   141	                        }
   142	                })
   143	        }
   144	}

   146	var cssInputs = []any{
   147	        []string{"a", "b"},          // []string
   148	        "c",                         // string
   149	        templ.ConstantCSSClass("d"), // ConstantCSSClass
   150	        templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "e", Class: ".e{color:red}"}, // ComponentCSSClass
   151	        map[string]bool{"f": true, "ff": false},                  // map[string]bool
   152	        templ.KV("g", true),                                      // KeyValue[string, bool]
   153	        templ.KV("gg", false),                                    // KeyValue[string, bool]
   154	        []templ.KeyValue[string, bool]{
   155	                templ.KV("h", true),
   156	                templ.KV("hh", false),
   157	        }, // []KeyValue[string, bool]
   158	        templ.KV(templ.ConstantCSSClass("i"), true),   // KeyValue[CSSClass, bool]
   159	        templ.KV(templ.ConstantCSSClass("ii"), false), // KeyValue[CSSClass, bool]
   160	        templ.KV(templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   161	                ID:    "j",
   162	                Class: ".j{color:red}",
   163	        }, true), // KeyValue[ComponentCSSClass, bool]
   164	        templ.KV(templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   165	                ID:    "jj",
   166	                Class: ".jj{color:red}",
   167	        }, false), // KeyValue[ComponentCSSClass, bool]
   168	        templ.CSSClasses{templ.ConstantCSSClass("k")},                // CSSClasses
   169	        func() templ.CSSClass { return templ.ConstantCSSClass("l") }, // func() CSSClass
   170	        templ.CSSClass(templ.ConstantCSSClass("m")),                  // CSSClass
   171	        customClass{name: "n"},                                       // CSSClass
   172	        []templ.CSSClass{customClass{name: "n"}},                     // []CSSClass
   173	        templ.KV(templ.ConstantCSSClass("o"), true),                  // KeyValue[ConstantCSSClass, bool]
   174	        []templ.KeyValue[templ.ConstantCSSClass, bool]{
   175	                templ.KV(templ.ConstantCSSClass("p"), true),
   176	                templ.KV(templ.ConstantCSSClass("pp"), false),
   177	        }, // []KeyValue[ConstantCSSClass, bool]
   178	}

   181	        name string
   182	}

   188	func TestRenderCSS(t *testing.T) {
   189	        c1 := templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   190	                ID:    "c1",
   191	                Class: ".c1{color:red}",
   192	        }
   193	        c2 := templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   194	                ID:    "c2",
   195	                Class: ".c2{color:blue}",
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        tests := []struct {
   199	                name     string
   200	                toIgnore []any
   201	                toRender []any
   202	                expected string
   203	        }{
   204	                {
   205	                        name:     "if none are ignored, everything is rendered",
   206	                        toIgnore: nil,
   207	                        toRender: []any{c1, c2},
   208	                        expected: `<style type="text/css">.c1{color:red}.c2{color:blue}</style>`,
   209	                },
   210	                {
   211	                        name: "if something outside the expected is ignored, if has no effect",
   212	                        toIgnore: []any{
   213	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   214	                                        ID:    "c3",
   215	                                        Class: templ.SafeCSS(".c3{color:yellow}"),
   216	                                },
   217	                        },
   218	                        toRender: []any{c1, c2},
   219	                        expected: `<style type="text/css">.c1{color:red}.c2{color:blue}</style>`,
   220	                },
   221	                {
   222	                        name:     "if one is ignored, it's not rendered",
   223	                        toIgnore: []any{c1},
   224	                        toRender: []any{c1, c2},
   225	                        expected: `<style type="text/css">.c2{color:blue}</style>`,
   226	                },
   227	                {
   228	                        name: "if all are ignored, not even style tags are rendered",
   229	                        toIgnore: []any{
   230	                                c1,
   231	                                c2,
   232	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   233	                                        ID:    "c3",
   234	                                        Class: templ.SafeCSS(".c3{color:yellow}"),
   235	                                },
   236	                        },
   237	                        toRender: []any{c1, c2},
   238	                        expected: ``,
   239	                },
   240	                {
   241	                        name:     "CSS classes are rendered",
   242	                        toIgnore: nil,
   243	                        toRender: cssInputs,
   244	                        expected: `<style type="text/css">.e{color:red}.j{color:red}</style>`,
   245	                },
   246	        }
   247	        for _, tt := range tests {
   248	                tt := tt
   249	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   250	                        ctx := context.Background()
   251	                        b := new(bytes.Buffer)
   252	
   253	                        // Render twice, reusing the same context so that there's a memory of which classes have been rendered.
   254	                        ctx = templ.InitializeContext(ctx)
   255	                        err := templ.RenderCSSItems(ctx, b, tt.toIgnore...)
   256	                        if err != nil {
   257	                                t.Fatalf("failed to render initial CSS: %v", err)
   258	                        }
   259	
   260	                        // Now render again to check that only the expected classes were rendered.
   261	                        b.Reset()
   262	                        err = templ.RenderCSSItems(ctx, b, tt.toRender...)
   263	                        if err != nil {
   264	                                t.Fatalf("failed to render CSS: %v", err)
   265	                        }
   266	
   267	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(tt.expected, b.String()); diff != "" {
   268	                                t.Error(diff)
   269	                        }
   270	                })
   271	        }
   272	}
   273	
   274	func TestRenderCSSItemsWithNonce(t *testing.T) {
   275	        ctx := templ.WithNonce(context.Background(), "testnonce")
   276	        b := new(bytes.Buffer)
   277	        c := templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   278	                ID:    "c1",
   279	                Class: ".c1{color:red}",
   280	        }
   281	        err := templ.RenderCSSItems(ctx, b, c)
   282	        if err != nil {
   283	                t.Fatalf("failed to render CSS: %v", err)
   284	        }
   285	        actual := b.String()
   286	        // Should include nonce attribute on <style> tag.
   287	        expected := `<style type="text/css" nonce="testnonce">.c1{color:red}</style>`
   288	        if actual != expected {
   289	                t.Errorf("expected %q, got %q", expected, actual)
   290	        }
   291	}

   293	func TestClassesFunction(t *testing.T) {
   294	        tests := []struct {
   295	                name     string
   296	                input    []any
   297	                expected string
   298	        }{
   299	                {
   300	                        name:     "constants are allowed",
   301	                        input:    []any{"a", "b", "c", "</style>"},
   302	                        expected: "a b c </style>",
   303	                },
   304	                {
   305	                        name:     "legacy CSS types are supported",
   306	                        input:    []any{"a", templ.SafeClass("b"), templ.Class("c")},
   307	                        expected: "a b c",
   308	                },
   309	                {
   310	                        name: "CSS components are included in the output",
   311	                        input: []any{
   312	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "classA", Class: templ.SafeCSS(".classA{background-color:white;}")},
   313	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "classB", Class: templ.SafeCSS(".classB{background-color:green;}")},
   314	                                "c",
   315	                        },
   316	                        expected: "classA classB c",
   317	                },
   318	                {
   319	                        name: "optional classes can be applied with expressions",
   320	                        input: []any{
   321	                                "a",
   322	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "classA", Class: templ.SafeCSS(".classA{background-color:white;}")},
   323	                                templ.ComponentCSSClass{ID: "classB", Class: templ.SafeCSS(".classB{background-color:green;}")},
   324	                                "c",
   325	                                map[string]bool{
   326	                                        "a":      false,
   327	                                        "classA": false,
   328	                                        "classB": false,
   329	                                        "c":      true,
   330	                                        "d":      false,
   331	                                },
   332	                        },
   333	                        expected: "c",
   334	                },
   335	                {
   336	                        name: "unknown types for classes get rendered as --templ-css-class-unknown-type",
   337	                        input: []any{
   338	                                123,
   339	                                map[string]string{"test": "no"},
   340	                                false,
   341	                                "c",
   342	                        },
   343	                        expected: "--templ-css-class-unknown-type c",
   344	                },
   345	                {
   346	                        name: "string arrays are supported",
   347	                        input: []any{
   348	                                []string{"a", "b", "c", "</style>"},
   349	                                "d",
   350	                        },
   351	                        expected: "a b c </style> d",
   352	                },
   353	                {
   354	                        name: "strings are broken up",
   355	                        input: []any{
   356	                                "a </style>",
   357	                        },
   358	                        expected: "a </style>",
   359	                },
   360	                {
   361	                        name: "if a templ.CSSClasses is passed in, the nested CSSClasses are extracted",
   362	                        input: []any{
   363	                                templ.Classes(
   364	                                        "a",
   365	                                        templ.SafeClass("b"),
   366	                                        templ.Class("c"),
   367	                                        templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   368	                                                ID:    "d",
   369	                                                Class: "{}",
   370	                                        },
   371	                                ),
   372	                        },
   373	                        expected: "a b c d",
   374	                },
   375	                {
   376	                        name: "kv types can be used to show or hide classes",
   377	                        input: []any{
   378	                                "a",
   379	                                templ.KV("b", true),
   380	                                "c",
   381	                                templ.KV("c", false),
   382	                                templ.KV(templ.SafeClass("d"), true),
   383	                                templ.KV(templ.SafeClass("e"), false),
   384	                        },
   385	                        expected: "a b d",
   386	                },
   387	                {
   388	                        name: "an array of KV types can be used to show or hide classes",
   389	                        input: []any{
   390	                                "a",
   391	                                "c",
   392	                                []templ.KeyValue[string, bool]{
   393	                                        templ.KV("b", true),
   394	                                        templ.KV("c", false),
   395	                                        {"d", true},
   396	                                },
   397	                        },
   398	                        expected: "a b d",
   399	                },
   400	                {

   404	                                        return templ.ComponentCSSClass{
   405	                                                ID:    "a",
   406	                                                Class: "",
   407	                                        }
   408	                                },
   409	                        },
   410	                        expected: "a",
   411	                },
   412	        }

   414	                t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   415	                        actual := templ.Classes(test.input...).String()
   416	                        if actual != test.expected {
   417	                                t.Errorf("expected %q, got %q", test.expected, actual)
   418	                        }
   419	                })
   420	        }

   423	type baseError struct {
   424	        Value int
   425	}
   426	
   427	func (baseError) Error() string { return "base error" }
   428	
   429	type nonMatchedError struct{}
   430	
   431	func (nonMatchedError) Error() string { return "non matched error" }
   432	
   433	func TestErrorWrapping(t *testing.T) {
   434	        baseErr := baseError{
   435	                Value: 1,
   436	        }
   437	        wrappedErr := templ.Error{Err: baseErr, Line: 1, Col: 2}
   438	        t.Run("errors.Is() returns true for the base error", func(t *testing.T) {
   439	                if !errors.Is(wrappedErr, baseErr) {
   440	                        t.Error("errors.Is() returned false for the base error")
   441	                }
   442	        })
   443	        t.Run("errors.Is() returns false for a different error", func(t *testing.T) {
   444	                if errors.Is(wrappedErr, errors.New("different error")) {
   445	                        t.Error("errors.Is() returned true for a different error")
   446	                }
   447	        })
   448	        t.Run("errors.As() returns true for the base error", func(t *testing.T) {
   449	                var err baseError
   450	                if !errors.As(wrappedErr, &err) {
   451	                        t.Error("errors.As() returned false for the base error")
   452	                }
   453	                if err.Value != 1 {
   454	                        t.Errorf("errors.As() returned a different value: %v", err.Value)
   455	                }
   456	        })
   457	        t.Run("errors.As() returns false for a different error", func(t *testing.T) {
   458	                var err nonMatchedError
   459	                if errors.As(wrappedErr, &err) {
   460	                        t.Error("errors.As() returned true for a different error")
   461	                }
   462	        })
   463	}
   464	
   465	func TestRawComponent(t *testing.T) {
   466	        tests := []struct {
   467	                name        string
   468	                input       templ.Component
   469	                expected    string
   470	                expectedErr error
   471	        }{
   472	                {
   473	                        name:     "Raw content is not escaped",
   474	                        input:    templ.Raw("<div>Test &</div>"),
   475	                        expected: `<div>Test &</div>`,
   476	                },
   477	                {
   478	                        name:        "Raw will return errors first",
   479	                        input:       templ.Raw("", nil, errors.New("test error")),
   480	                        expected:    `<div>Test &</div>`,
   481	                        expectedErr: errors.New("test error"),
   482	                },
   483	                {
   484	                        name:     "Strings marked as safe are rendered without escaping",
   485	                        input:    templ.Raw(template.HTML("<div>")),
   486	                        expected: `<div>`,
   487	                },
   488	        }
   489	        for _, tt := range tests {
   490	                tt := tt
   491	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   492	                        b := new(bytes.Buffer)
   493	                        err := tt.input.Render(context.Background(), b)
   494	                        if tt.expectedErr != nil {
   495	                                expected := tt.expectedErr.Error()
   496	                                actual := fmt.Sprintf("%v", err)
   497	                                if actual != expected {
   498	                                        t.Errorf("expected error %q, got %q", expected, actual)
   499	                                }
   500	                                return
   501	                        }
   502	                        if err != nil {
   503	                                t.Fatalf("failed to render content: %v", err)
   504	                        }
   505	                        if diff := cmp.Diff(tt.expected, b.String()); diff != "" {
   506	                                t.Error(diff)
   507	                        }
   508	                })
   509	        }
   510	        t.Run("Raw does not require allocations", func(t *testing.T) {
   511	                actualAllocs := testing.AllocsPerRun(4, func() {
   512	                        c := templ.Raw("<div>")
   513	                        if c == nil {
   514	                                t.Fatalf("unexpected nil value")
   515	                        }
   516	                })
   517	                if actualAllocs > 0 {
   518	                        t.Errorf("expected no allocs, got %v", actualAllocs)
   519	                }
   520	        })
   521	}

   523	var goTemplate = template.Must(template.New("example").Parse("<div>{{ . }}</div>"))
   524	
   525	func TestGoHTMLComponents(t *testing.T) {
   526	        t.Run("Go templates can be rendered as templ components", func(t *testing.T) {
   527	                b := new(bytes.Buffer)
   528	                err := templ.FromGoHTML(goTemplate, "Test &").Render(context.Background(), b)
   529	                if err != nil {
   530	                        t.Fatalf("failed to render content: %v", err)
   531	                }
   532	                if diff := cmp.Diff("<div>Test &amp;</div>", b.String()); diff != "" {
   533	                        t.Error(diff)
   534	                }
   535	        })
   536	        t.Run("templ components can be rendered in Go templates", func(t *testing.T) {
   537	                b := new(bytes.Buffer)
   538	                c := templ.ComponentFunc(func(ctx context.Context, w io.Writer) (err error) {
   539	                        _, err = io.WriteString(w, "<div>Unsanitized &</div>")
   540	                        return err
   541	                })
   542	                h, err := templ.ToGoHTML(context.Background(), c)
   543	                if err != nil {
   544	                        t.Fatalf("failed to convert to Go HTML: %v", err)
   545	                }
   546	                if err = goTemplate.Execute(b, h); err != nil {
   547	                        t.Fatalf("failed to render content: %v", err)
   548	                }
   549	                if diff := cmp.Diff("<div><div>Unsanitized &</div></div>", b.String()); diff != "" {
   550	                        t.Error(diff)
   551	                }
   552	        })
   553	        t.Run("errors in ToGoHTML are returned", func(t *testing.T) {

   555	                c := templ.ComponentFunc(func(ctx context.Context, w io.Writer) (err error) {
   556	                        return expectedErr
   557	                })

   560	                        t.Fatalf("expected error, got nil")

   563	                        t.Fatalf("expected error %q, got %q", expectedErr, err)
   564	                }
   565	        })
   566	        t.Run("FromGoHTML does not require allocations", func(t *testing.T) {
   567	                actualAllocs := testing.AllocsPerRun(4, func() {
   568	                        c := templ.FromGoHTML(goTemplate, "test &")
   569	                        if c == nil {

import (
	"context"
	"strings"
	"testing"

	"github.com/a-h/templ"
)

func TestRenderAttributesWithNonStringValues(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name     string
		attrs    templ.Attributes
		expected string
	}{
		{
			name: "integer attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": 42,
			},
			expected: ` type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "float attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":    "number",
				"step":    0.5,
				"max":     100.0,
			},
			expected: ` max="100" step="0.5" type="number"`,
		},
		{
			name: "mixed types",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":     "text",
				"value":    42,
				"disabled": true,
				"data-id":  "test123",
			},
			expected: ` data-id="test123" disabled type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "nil pointer should be ignored",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": (*int)(nil),
			},
			expected: ` type="text"`,
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			var buf strings.Builder
			err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, tt.attrs)
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("RenderAttributes failed: %v", err)
			}
			
			result := buf.String()
			if result != tt.expected {
				t.Errorf("Expected %q but got %q", tt.expected, result)
			}
		})
	}
}'

Now I understand the issue. The `RenderAttributes` function only handles specific types in its `switch` statement (strings, pointers to strings, booleans, pointers to booleans, certain `KeyValue` types, and `func() bool`). It doesn't have a default case or handling for other types like integers, floats, etc.

Based on the PR description mentioning `fmt.Sprint`, I need to add a default case that uses `fmt.Sprint` to convert any unknown type to a string.

Let me implement the fix:



🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/runtime.go   --old_str 'func RenderAttributes(ctx context.Context, w io.Writer, attributes Attributer) (err error) {
        for _, item := range attributes.Items() {
                key := item.Key
                value := item.Value
                switch value := value.(type) {
                case string:
                        if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(value), `"`); err != nil {
                                return err
                        }
                case *string:
                        if value != nil {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(*value), `"`); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case bool:
                        if value {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case *bool:
                        if value != nil && *value {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case KeyValue[string, bool]:
                        if value.Value {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(value.Key), `"`); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case KeyValue[bool, bool]:
                        if value.Value && value.Key {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case func() bool:
                        if value() {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                }
        }
        return nil
}' --new_str 'func RenderAttributes(ctx context.Context, w io.Writer, attributes Attributer) (err error) {
        for _, item := range attributes.Items() {
                key := item.Key
                value := item.Value
                switch value := value.(type) {
                case string:
                        if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(value), `"`); err != nil {
                                return err
                        }
                case *string:
                        if value != nil {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(*value), `"`); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case bool:
                        if value {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case *bool:
                        if value != nil && *value {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case KeyValue[string, bool]:
                        if value.Value {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(value.Key), `"`); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case KeyValue[bool, bool]:
                        if value.Value && value.Key {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                case func() bool:
                        if value() {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key)); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                default:
                        // Handle any other type by converting to string using fmt.Sprint
                        if value != nil {
                                if err = writeStrings(w, ` `, EscapeString(key), `="`, EscapeString(fmt.Sprint(value)), `"`); err != nil {
                                        return err
                                }
                        }
                }
        }
        return nil

func TestRenderAttributesWithNonStringValues(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name     string
		attrs    templ.Attributes
		expected string
	}{
		{
			name: "integer attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": 42,
			},
			expected: ` type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "float attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":    "number",
				"step":    0.5,
				"max":     100.0,
			},
			expected: ` max="100" step="0.5" type="number"`,
		},
		{
			name: "mixed types",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":     "text",
				"value":    42,
				"disabled": true,
				"data-id":  "test123",
			},
			expected: ` data-id="test123" disabled type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "nil pointer should be ignored",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": (*int)(nil),
			},
			expected: ` type="text"`,
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			var buf strings.Builder
			err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, tt.attrs)
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("RenderAttributes failed: %v", err)
			}
			
			result := buf.String()
			if result != tt.expected {
				t.Errorf("Expected %q but got %q", tt.expected, result)
			}
		})
	}
}'

func TestRenderAttributesWithNonStringValues(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name     string
		attrs    templ.Attributes
		expected string
	}{
		{
			name: "integer attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": 42,
			},
			expected: ` type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "float attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":    "number",
				"step":    0.5,
				"max":     100.0,
			},
			expected: ` max="100" step="0.5" type="number"`,
		},
		{
			name: "mixed types",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":     "text",
				"value":    42,
				"disabled": true,
				"data-id":  "test123",
			},
			expected: ` data-id="test123" disabled type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "nil pointer should be ignored",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": (*int)(nil),
			},
			expected: ` type="text"`,
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			var buf strings.Builder
			err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, tt.attrs)
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("RenderAttributes failed: %v", err)
			}
			
			result := buf.String()
			if result != tt.expected {
				t.Errorf("Expected %q but got %q", tt.expected, result)
			}
		})
	}
}'

func TestRenderAttributesWithNonStringValues(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name     string
		attrs    templ.Attributes
		expected string
	}{
		{
			name: "integer attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": 42,
			},
			expected: ` type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "float attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":    "number",
				"step":    0.5,
				"max":     100.0,
			},
			expected: ` max="100" step="0.5" type="number"`,
		},
		{
			name: "mixed types",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":     "text",
				"value":    42,
				"disabled": true,
				"data-id":  "test123",
			},
			expected: ` data-id="test123" disabled type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "nil pointer should be ignored",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": (*int)(nil),
			},
			expected: ` type="text"`,
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			var buf strings.Builder
			err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, tt.attrs)
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("RenderAttributes failed: %v", err)
			}
			
			result := buf.String()
			if result != tt.expected {
				t.Errorf("Expected %q but got %q", tt.expected, result)
			}
		})
	}
}'

func TestNonce(t *testing.T) {
	ctx := context.Background()
	t.Run("returns empty string if not set", func(t *testing.T) {
		actual := templ.GetNonce(ctx)
		if actual != "" {
			t.Errorf("expected empty string got %q", actual)
		}
	})
	t.Run("returns value if one has been set", func(t *testing.T) {
		expected := "abc123"
		ctx := templ.WithNonce(context.Background(), expected)
		actual := templ.GetNonce(ctx)
		if actual != expected {
			t.Errorf("expected %q got %q", expected, actual)
		}
	})
}

func TestRenderAttributesWithNonStringValues(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []struct {
		name     string
		attrs    templ.Attributes
		expected string
	}{
		{
			name: "integer attribute value",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":  "text",
				"value": 42,
			},
			expected: ` type="text" value="42"`,
		},
		{
			name: "mixed types",
			attrs: templ.Attributes{
				"type":     "text",
				"value":    42,
				"disabled": true,
				"data-id":  "test123",
			},
			expected: ` data-id="test123" disabled type="text" value="42"`,
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			var buf strings.Builder
			err := templ.RenderAttributes(context.Background(), &buf, tt.attrs)
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatalf("RenderAttributes failed: %v", err)
			}
			
			result := buf.String()
			if result != tt.expected {
				t.Errorf("Expected %q but got %q", tt.expected, result)
			}
		})
	}
}'
